### [214] [Observations and Remedies for Large Language Model Bias in Self-Consuming Performative Loop](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.05184)
*Yaxuan Wang,Zhongteng Cai,Yujia Bao,Xueru Zhang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究提出自消耗执行循环(SCPL)概念，探讨在受控执行反馈下合成数据如何影响动态迭代训练过程中的偏见演变，发现执行循环会增加偏好偏见但减少差异偏见，并提出基于奖励的拒绝采样策略来缓解偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型的快速发展导致使用合成数据训练未来模型的兴趣增长，但这会形成自消耗的再训练循环，可能导致性能下降和偏见涌现。现实应用中，先前部署的LLM可能影响其生成的数据，形成由用户反馈驱动的动态系统。由于无法获取动态生产系统中的真实用户偏好数据，需要建立受控环境来隔离和分析反馈驱动的偏见演变。

Method: 引入自消耗执行循环(SCPL)概念，在受控执行反馈下研究合成数据如何影响动态迭代训练过程中的偏见演变。研究两种循环类型：典型的再训练设置和增量微调设置。通过三个真实世界任务的实验，分析偏见演变，并设计基于奖励的拒绝采样策略来缓解偏见。

Result: 实验发现执行循环会增加偏好偏见但减少差异偏见。基于奖励的拒绝采样策略能够有效缓解偏见，推动构建更可信的自改进系统。

Conclusion: 自消耗执行循环在动态迭代训练中会显著影响偏见演变，需要设计专门的缓解策略。提出的基于奖励的拒绝采样方法为构建更可信的自改进系统提供了有效途径，有助于理解和管理合成数据训练中的偏见问题。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) has led to growing interest in using synthetic data to train future models. However, this creates a self-consuming retraining loop, where models are trained on their own outputs and may cause performance drops and induce emerging biases. In real-world applications, previously deployed LLMs may influence the data they generate, leading to a dynamic system driven by user feedback. For example, if a model continues to underserve users from a group, less query data will be collected from this particular demographic of users. In this study, we introduce the concept of \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{C}onsuming \textbf{P}erformative \textbf{L}oop (\textbf{SCPL}) and investigate the role of synthetic data in shaping bias during these dynamic iterative training processes under controlled performative feedback. This controlled setting is motivated by the inaccessibility of real-world user preference data from dynamic production systems, and enables us to isolate and analyze feedback-driven bias evolution in a principled manner. We focus on two types of loops, including the typical retraining setting and the incremental fine-tuning setting, which is largely underexplored. Through experiments on three real-world tasks, we find that the performative loop increases preference bias and decreases disparate bias. We design a reward-based rejection sampling strategy to mitigate the bias, moving towards more trustworthy self-improving systems.

### [216] [Intraday Limit Order Price Change Transition Dynamics Across Market Capitalizations Through Markov Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.04959)
*Salam Rabindrajit Luwang,Kundan Mukhia,Buddha Nath Sharma,Md. Nurujjaman,Anish Rai,Filippo Petroni*

Main category: q-fin.ST

TL;DR: 该研究使用离散时间马尔可夫链分析纳斯达克100指数成分股的高频数据，发现价格惯性在开盘和收盘时段最强，中午趋于稳定，且高市值股票表现出最强的价格惯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解限价单价格变化的随机动力学对于执行策略设计至关重要，特别是不同市值股票在日内不同时段的价格动态模式。

Method: 使用离散时间马尔可夫链框架，将连续价格变化分为9个状态，为高、中、低市值股票在6个日内时段估计转移概率矩阵，并应用谱隙、熵率、平均复发时间等马尔可夫指标进行分析。

Result: 发现价格惯性在开盘和收盘时段达到峰值，中午趋于稳定；高市值股票表现出最强的惯性，低市值股票稳定性较低且价差更宽；聚类分析识别出买卖双方不同的时间阶段模式。

Conclusion: 限价单动态主要由中性温和的价格变化主导，收盘时段是最独特的阶段，市值调节时间对比和买卖不对称性，这些发现支持基于市值感知和时间自适应的执行算法。

Abstract: Quantitative understanding of stochastic dynamics in limit order price changes is essential for execution strategy design. We analyze intraday transition dynamics of ask and bid orders across market capitalization tiers using high-frequency NASDAQ100 tick data. Employing a discrete-time Markov chain framework, we categorize consecutive price changes into nine states and estimate transition probability matrices (TPMs) for six intraday intervals across High ($\mathtt{HMC}$), Medium ($\mathtt{MMC}$), and Low ($\mathtt{LMC}$) market cap stocks. Element-wise TPM comparison reveals systematic patterns: price inertia peaks during opening and closing hours, stabilizing midday. A capitalization gradient is observed: $\mathtt{HMC}$ stocks exhibit the strongest inertia, while $\mathtt{LMC}$ stocks show lower stability and wider spreads. Markov metrics, including spectral gap, entropy rate, and mean recurrence times, quantify these dynamics. Clustering analysis identifies three distinct temporal phases on the bid side -- Opening, Midday, and Closing, and four phases on the ask side by distinguishing Opening, Midday, Pre-Close, and Close. This indicates that sellers initiate end-of-day positioning earlier than buyers. Stationary distributions show limit order dynamics are dominated by neutral and mild price changes. Jensen-Shannon divergence confirms the closing hour as the most distinct phase, with capitalization modulating temporal contrasts and bid-ask asymmetry. These findings support capitalization-aware and time-adaptive execution algorithms.

### [217] [Trading Electrons: Predicting DART Spread Spikes in ISO Electricity Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.05085)
*Emma Hubert,Dimitrios Lolas,Ronnie Sircar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Galarneau-Vincent等人的框架，将尖峰预测扩展到多区域设置，统一处理正负DART尖峰。开发基于日前报价堆栈的结构化市场一致性价格影响模型，推导出区域INC/DEC数量的最优向量闭式解，捕捉不对称买卖影响和跨区域阻塞效应。

Result: 在NYISO市场应用中，考虑价格影响的策略显著改善了风险收益特征，相对于单位规模交易有明显提升，并揭示了不同市场和季节间的显著异质性。

Abstract: We study the problem of forecasting and optimally trading day-ahead versus real-time (DART) price spreads in U.S. wholesale electricity markets. Building on the framework of Galarneau-Vincent et al., we extend spike prediction from a single zone to a multi-zone setting and treat both positive and negative DART spikes within a unified statistical model. To translate directional signals into economically meaningful positions, we develop a structural and market-consistent price impact model based on day-ahead bid stacks. This yields closed-form expressions for the optimal vector of zonal INC/DEC quantities, capturing asymmetric buy/sell impacts and cross-zone congestion effects. When applied to NYISO, the resulting impact-aware strategy significantly improves the risk-return profile relative to unit-size trading and highlights substantial heterogeneity across markets and seasons.

</details>
